Deterministic: ()
()]
  (: is-variable 
    (-> Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (is-variable $x) 
    (== 
      (get-metatype $x) Variable))
  (: lazy-or 
    (-> Bool Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (lazy-or False $x) $x)
  (= 
    (lazy-or True $x) True)
  (: is-expression 
    (-> Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (is-expression $x) 
    (== 
      (get-metatype $x) Expression))
  (: is-closed 
    (-> Atom Bool))
  (= 
    (is-closed $x) 
    (if 
      (is-variable $x) False 
      (if 
        (== () $x) True 
        (if 
          (is-expression $x) 
          (and 
            (let $head 
              (car-atom $x) 
              (is-closed $head)) 
            (let $tail 
              (cdr-atom $x) 
              (is-closed $tail))) True))))
